\subsubsection[{C\-U\-\_\-p\-Test\-Info}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}typedef {\bf C\-U\-\_\-\-Test\-Info}$\ast$ {\bf C\-U\-\_\-p\-Test\-Info}}}\label{group__Framework_ga146a57ac2abef6382399be83afb1daed}

\hypertarget{group__Framework_gaccf591ac5a134c3ba3a1becb7d469094}{\index{Framework@{Framework}!C\-U\-\_\-\-Run\-Summary@{C\-U\-\_\-\-Run\-Summary}}
\index{C\-U\-\_\-\-Run\-Summary@{C\-U\-\_\-\-Run\-Summary}!Framework@{Framework}}
\subsubsection[{C\-U\-\_\-\-Run\-Summary}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}typedef struct {\bf C\-U\-\_\-\-Run\-Summary}  {\bf C\-U\-\_\-\-Run\-Summary}}}\label{group__Framework_gaccf591ac5a134c3ba3a1becb7d469094}


Data type for holding statistics and assertion failures for a test run. 

\hypertarget{group__Framework_gad58d2b18d7da9c0ae48ae1679d1b8861}{\index{Framework@{Framework}!C\-U\-\_\-\-Suite@{C\-U\-\_\-\-Suite}}
\index{C\-U\-\_\-\-Suite@{C\-U\-\_\-\-Suite}!Framework@{Framework}}
\subsubsection[{C\-U\-\_\-\-Suite}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}typedef struct {\bf C\-U\-\_\-\-Suite}  {\bf C\-U\-\_\-\-Suite}}}\label{group__Framework_gad58d2b18d7da9c0ae48ae1679d1b8861}


C\-Unit suite data type. 

\hyperlink{structCU__Suite}{C\-U\-\_\-\-Suite} is a linked list of \hyperlink{structCU__Test}{C\-U\-\_\-\-Test} containers. Each suite has a name, a count of registered unit tests, and a flag for whether the suite is active during test runs. It also holds pointers to optional initialization and cleanup functions. If non-\/\-N\-U\-L\-L, these are called before and after running the suite's tests, respectively. In addition, the suite holds a pointer to the head of the linked list of associated \hyperlink{structCU__Test}{C\-U\-\_\-\-Test} objects. Finally, pointers to the next and previous suites in the linked list are maintained.\par
\par


Generally, the linked list includes suites which are associated with each other in a \hyperlink{structCU__TestRegistry}{C\-U\-\_\-\-Test\-Registry}. As a result, suites are run in the order in which they are registered (see \hyperlink{group__Framework_ga94b8f1bbbd93b154a60bb1d43391b48a}{C\-U\-\_\-add\-\_\-suite()}).\par
\par


It is recommended that name of each \hyperlink{structCU__Suite}{C\-U\-\_\-\-Suite} in a test registry have a unique name. Otherwise, only the first-\/registered suite having a given name will be accessible by name. There are no restrictions on the contained tests. This means that the same \hyperlink{structCU__Test}{C\-U\-\_\-\-Test} could, in principle, be run more than once fron different suites.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{Voir également}
\hyperlink{structCU__Test}{C\-U\-\_\-\-Test} 

\hyperlink{structCU__TestRegistry}{C\-U\-\_\-\-Test\-Registry} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\hypertarget{group__Framework_ga67a720062975e6b7f97df16a1e8e10ce}{\index{Framework@{Framework}!C\-U\-\_\-\-Suite\-Cleanup\-Failure\-Message\-Handler@{C\-U\-\_\-\-Suite\-Cleanup\-Failure\-Message\-Handler}}
\index{C\-U\-\_\-\-Suite\-Cleanup\-Failure\-Message\-Handler@{C\-U\-\_\-\-Suite\-Cleanup\-Failure\-Message\-Handler}!Framework@{Framework}}
\subsubsection[{C\-U\-\_\-\-Suite\-Cleanup\-Failure\-Message\-Handler}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}typedef void($\ast$ C\-U\-\_\-\-Suite\-Cleanup\-Failure\-Message\-Handler)(const {\bf C\-U\-\_\-p\-Suite} p\-Suite)}}\label{group__Framework_ga67a720062975e6b7f97df16a1e8e10ce}


Message handler called when a suite cleanup function fails. 

The test run is considered in progress when the message handler is called. \hypertarget{group__Framework_gafe19dbdf8b13029d10e9463bc698be58}{\index{Framework@{Framework}!C\-U\-\_\-\-Suite\-Complete\-Message\-Handler@{C\-U\-\_\-\-Suite\-Complete\-Message\-Handler}}
\index{C\-U\-\_\-\-Suite\-Complete\-Message\-Handler@{C\-U\-\_\-\-Suite\-Complete\-Message\-Handler}!Framework@{Framework}}
\subsubsection[{C\-U\-\_\-\-Suite\-Complete\-Message\-Handler}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}typedef void($\ast$ C\-U\-\_\-\-Suite\-Complete\-Message\-Handler)(const {\bf C\-U\-\_\-p\-Suite} p\-Suite, const {\bf C\-U\-\_\-p\-Failure\-Record} p\-Failure)}}\label{group__Framework_gafe19dbdf8b13029d10e9463bc698be58}


Message handler called at the completion of a suite. 

The parameters are suite being run, plus a pointer to the first failure record applicable to this suite. If the suite and it's tests did not have any failures, p\-Failure will be N\-U\-L\-L. The test run is considered in progress when the message handler is called. \hypertarget{group__Framework_ga345177d10f56a80873124d47cae930f0}{\index{Framework@{Framework}!C\-U\-\_\-\-Suite\-Info@{C\-U\-\_\-\-Suite\-Info}}
\index{C\-U\-\_\-\-Suite\-Info@{C\-U\-\_\-\-Suite\-Info}!Framework@{Framework}}
\subsubsection[{C\-U\-\_\-\-Suite\-Info}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}typedef struct {\bf C\-U\-\_\-\-Suite\-Info}  {\bf C\-U\-\_\-\-Suite\-Info}}}\label{group__Framework_ga345177d10f56a80873124d47cae930f0}


Suite parameters. 

This data type is provided to assist C\-Unit users manage collections of tests and suites. It is intended to be used to build arrays of suite parameters that can be passed to a bulk registration function such as C\-U\-\_\-register\-\_\-suite() or \hyperlink{group__Framework_ga331001da0a8bd8faececdb48e7ad3f96}{C\-U\-\_\-register\-\_\-suites()}. \hypertarget{group__Framework_ga53faf49a6045a1fc32c5a0287b800b65}{\index{Framework@{Framework}!C\-U\-\_\-\-Suite\-Init\-Failure\-Message\-Handler@{C\-U\-\_\-\-Suite\-Init\-Failure\-Message\-Handler}}
\index{C\-U\-\_\-\-Suite\-Init\-Failure\-Message\-Handler@{C\-U\-\_\-\-Suite\-Init\-Failure\-Message\-Handler}!Framework@{Framework}}
\subsubsection[{C\-U\-\_\-\-Suite\-Init\-Failure\-Message\-Handler}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}typedef void($\ast$ C\-U\-\_\-\-Suite\-Init\-Failure\-Message\-Handler)(const {\bf C\-U\-\_\-p\-Suite} p\-Suite)}}\label{group__Framework_ga53faf49a6045a1fc32c5a0287b800b65}


Message handler called when a suite initializer fails. 

The test run is considered in progress when the message handler is called. \hypertarget{group__Framework_gab7f4df4360e8d2faa7e59571a1409448}{\index{Framework@{Framework}!C\-U\-\_\-\-Suite\-Start\-Message\-Handler@{C\-U\-\_\-\-Suite\-Start\-Message\-Handler}}
\index{C\-U\-\_\-\-Suite\-Start\-Message\-Handler@{C\-U\-\_\-\-Suite\-Start\-Message\-Handler}!Framework@{Framework}}
\subsubsection[{C\-U\-\_\-\-Suite\-Start\-Message\-Handler}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}typedef void($\ast$ C\-U\-\_\-\-Suite\-Start\-Message\-Handler)(const {\bf C\-U\-\_\-p\-Suite} p\-Suite)}}\label{group__Framework_gab7f4df4360e8d2faa7e59571a1409448}


Message handler called at the start of a suite. 

p\-Suite will not be null. \hypertarget{group__Framework_ga0bc6468b9781a574e2c7994ca700ee1e}{\index{Framework@{Framework}!C\-U\-\_\-\-Test@{C\-U\-\_\-\-Test}}
\index{C\-U\-\_\-\-Test@{C\-U\-\_\-\-Test}!Framework@{Framework}}
\subsubsection[{C\-U\-\_\-\-Test}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}typedef struct {\bf C\-U\-\_\-\-Test}  {\bf C\-U\-\_\-\-Test}}}\label{group__Framework_ga0bc6468b9781a574e2c7994ca700ee1e}


C\-Unit test case data type. 

\hyperlink{structCU__Test}{C\-U\-\_\-\-Test} is a double linked list of unit tests. Each test has a name, a callable test function, and a flag for whether the test is active and thus executed during a test run. A test also holds links to the next and previous tests in the list, as well as a jmp\-\_\-buf reference for use in implementing fatal assertions.\par
\par


Generally, the linked list includes tests which are associated with each other in a \hyperlink{structCU__Suite}{C\-U\-\_\-\-Suite}. As a result, tests are run in the order in which they are added to a suite (see \hyperlink{group__Framework_gad9f198a8a5fa8cc6870c3c8be873869f}{C\-U\-\_\-add\-\_\-test()}). \par
\par


It is recommended that the name of each \hyperlink{structCU__Test}{C\-U\-\_\-\-Test} in a suite have a unique name. Otherwise, only the first-\/registered test having a given name will be accessible by that name. There are no restrictions on the test function. This means that the same function could, in principle, be called more than once from different tests.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{Voir également}
\hyperlink{structCU__Suite}{C\-U\-\_\-\-Suite} 

\hyperlink{structCU__TestRegistry}{C\-U\-\_\-\-Test\-Registry} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\hypertarget{group__Framework_ga2c11da75531b097ca037223489bf02be}{\index{Framework@{Framework}!C\-U\-\_\-\-Test\-Complete\-Message\-Handler@{C\-U\-\_\-\-Test\-Complete\-Message\-Handler}}
\index{C\-U\-\_\-\-Test\-Complete\-Message\-Handler@{C\-U\-\_\-\-Test\-Complete\-Message\-Handler}!Framework@{Framework}}
\subsubsection[{C\-U\-\_\-\-Test\-Complete\-Message\-Handler}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}typedef void($\ast$ C\-U\-\_\-\-Test\-Complete\-Message\-Handler)(const {\bf C\-U\-\_\-p\-Test} p\-Test, const {\bf C\-U\-\_\-p\-Suite} p\-Suite, const {\bf C\-U\-\_\-p\-Failure\-Record} p\-Failure)}}\label{group__Framework_ga2c11da75531b097ca037223489bf02be}


Message handler called at the completion of a test. 

The parameters are the test and suite being run, plus a pointer to the first failure record applicable to this test. If the test did not have any assertion failures, p\-Failure will be N\-U\-L\-L. The test run is considered in progress when the message handler is called. \hypertarget{group__Framework_ga5868148b642b30635b8fe7f095c5b493}{\index{Framework@{Framework}!C\-U\-\_\-\-Test\-Func@{C\-U\-\_\-\-Test\-Func}}
\index{C\-U\-\_\-\-Test\-Func@{C\-U\-\_\-\-Test\-Func}!Framework@{Framework}}
\subsubsection[{C\-U\-\_\-\-Test\-Func}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}typedef void($\ast$ C\-U\-\_\-\-Test\-Func)(void)}}\label{group__Framework_ga5868148b642b30635b8fe7f095c5b493}


Signature for a testing function in a test case. 

\hypertarget{group__Framework_gad5892aef99bf82d4be23b9284531382d}{\index{Framework@{Framework}!C\-U\-\_\-\-Test\-Info@{C\-U\-\_\-\-Test\-Info}}
\index{C\-U\-\_\-\-Test\-Info@{C\-U\-\_\-\-Test\-Info}!Framework@{Framework}}
\subsubsection[{C\-U\-\_\-\-Test\-Info}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}typedef struct {\bf C\-U\-\_\-\-Test\-Info}  {\bf C\-U\-\_\-\-Test\-Info}}}\label{group__Framework_gad5892aef99bf82d4be23b9284531382d}


Test case parameters structure. 

This data type is provided to assist C\-Unit users manage collections of tests and suites. It is intended to be used to build arrays of test case parameters that can be then be referred to in a C\-U\-\_\-suite\-\_\-info\-\_\-t variable. \hypertarget{group__Framework_ga9a7758811da313b88b23c6e6fdc537a0}{\index{Framework@{Framework}!C\-U\-\_\-\-Test\-Registry@{C\-U\-\_\-\-Test\-Registry}}
\index{C\-U\-\_\-\-Test\-Registry@{C\-U\-\_\-\-Test\-Registry}!Framework@{Framework}}
\subsubsection[{C\-U\-\_\-\-Test\-Registry}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}typedef struct {\bf C\-U\-\_\-\-Test\-Registry}  {\bf C\-U\-\_\-\-Test\-Registry}}}\label{group__Framework_ga9a7758811da313b88b23c6e6fdc537a0}


C\-Unit test registry data type. 

C\-U\-\_\-\-Test\-Registy is the repository for suites containing unit tests. The test registry maintains a count of the number of \hyperlink{structCU__Suite}{C\-U\-\_\-\-Suite} objects contained in the registry, as well as a count of the total number of \hyperlink{structCU__Test}{C\-U\-\_\-\-Test} objects associated with those suites. It also holds a pointer to the head of the linked list of \hyperlink{structCU__Suite}{C\-U\-\_\-\-Suite} objects. \par
\par


With this structure, the user will normally add suites implictly to the internal test registry using \hyperlink{group__Framework_ga94b8f1bbbd93b154a60bb1d43391b48a}{C\-U\-\_\-add\-\_\-suite()}, and then add tests to each suite using \hyperlink{group__Framework_gad9f198a8a5fa8cc6870c3c8be873869f}{C\-U\-\_\-add\-\_\-test()}. Test runs are then initiated using one of the appropriate functions in Test\-Run.\-c via one of the user interfaces.\par
\par


Automatic creation and destruction of the internal registry and its objects is available using \hyperlink{group__Framework_ga3477b2d3e57c8f8aba36bbbdfa54920d}{C\-U\-\_\-initialize\-\_\-registry()} and \hyperlink{group__Framework_ga183eb7d7f79e149c767237cfef52cb82}{C\-U\-\_\-cleanup\-\_\-registry()}, respectively. For internal and testing purposes, the internal registry can be retrieved and assigned. Functions are also provided for creating and destroying independent registries.\par
\par


Note that earlier versions of C\-Unit also contained a pointer to a linked list of \hyperlink{structCU__FailureRecord}{C\-U\-\_\-\-Failure\-Record} objects (termed \-\_\-\-Test\-Results). This has been removed from theregistry and relocated to Test\-Run.\-c.

\hypertarget{group__Framework_ga3330df7f5c95933f4ba21c648933c928}{\index{Framework@{Framework}!C\-U\-\_\-\-Test\-Start\-Message\-Handler@{C\-U\-\_\-\-Test\-Start\-Message\-Handler}}

\subsubsection[{C\-U\-\_\-\-Test\-Start\-Message\-Handler}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}typedef void($\ast$ C\-U\-\_\-\-Test\-Start\-Message\-Handler)(const {\bf C\-U\-\_\-p\-Test} p\-Test, const {\bf C\-U\-\_\-p\-Suite} p\-Suite)}}\label{group__Framework_ga3330df7f5c95933f4ba21c648933c928}


Message handler called at the start of a test. 

The parameters are the test and suite being run. The test run is considered in progress when the message handler is called. Neither p\-Test nor p\-Suite may be null.

\subsection{Documentation des fonctions}
\hypertarget{group__Framework_ga94b8f1bbbd93b154a60bb1d43391b48a}{\index{Framework@{Framework}!C\-U\-\_\-add\-\_\-suite@{C\-U\-\_\-add\-\_\-suite}}
\index{C\-U\-\_\-add\-\_\-suite@{C\-U\-\_\-add\-\_\-suite}!Framework@{Framework}}
\subsubsection[{C\-U\-\_\-add\-\_\-suite}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}C\-U\-\_\-\-E\-X\-P\-O\-R\-T {\bf C\-U\-\_\-p\-Suite} C\-U\-\_\-add\-\_\-suite (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{const char $\ast$}]{str\-Name, }
\item[{{\bf C\-U\-\_\-\-Initialize\-Func}}]{p\-Init, }
\item[{{\bf C\-U\-\_\-\-Cleanup\-Func}}]{p\-Clean}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{group__Framework_ga94b8f1bbbd93b154a60bb1d43391b48a}


Creates a new test suite and adds it to the test registry. 

This function creates a new test suite having the specified name and initialization/cleanup functions and adds it to the test registry. The new suite will be active and able to be executed during a test run. The test registry must be initialized before calling this function (checked by assertion). p\-Init and p\-Clean may be N\-U\-L\-L, in which case no corresponding initialization of cleanup function will be called when the suite is run. str\-Name may be empty (\char`\"{}\char`\"{}) but may not be N\-U\-L\-L.\par
\par


The return value is a pointer to the newly-\/created suite, or N\-U\-L\-L if there was a problem with the suite creation or addition. An error code is also set for the framework. Note that if the name specified for the new suite is a duplicate, the suite will be created and added but the error code will be set to C\-U\-E\-\_\-\-D\-U\-P\-\_\-\-S\-U\-I\-T\-E. The duplicate suite will not be accessible by name.\par
\par


N\-O\-T\-E -\/ the C\-U\-\_\-p\-Suite pointer returned should N\-O\-T B\-E F\-R\-E\-E\-D B\-Y T\-H\-E U\-S\-E\-R. The suite is freed by the C\-Unit system when \hyperlink{group__Framework_ga183eb7d7f79e149c767237cfef52cb82}{C\-U\-\_\-cleanup\-\_\-registry()} is called. {\bfseries This function must not be called during a test run (checked by assertion)}. \par
\par


\hyperlink{group__Framework_ga94b8f1bbbd93b154a60bb1d43391b48a}{C\-U\-\_\-add\-\_\-suite()} sets the following error codes\-:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item C\-U\-E\-\_\-\-S\-U\-C\-C\-E\-S\-S if no errors occurred.
\item C\-U\-E\-\_\-\-N\-O\-R\-E\-G\-I\-S\-T\-R\-Y if the registry has not been initialized.
\item C\-U\-E\-\_\-\-N\-O\-\_\-\-S\-U\-I\-T\-E\-N\-A\-M\-E if str\-Name is N\-U\-L\-L.
\item C\-U\-E\-\_\-\-D\-U\-P\-\_\-\-S\-U\-I\-T\-E if a suite having str\-Name is already registered.
\item C\-U\-E\-\_\-\-N\-O\-M\-E\-M\-O\-R\-Y if a memory allocation failed.
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Paramètres}
{\em str\-Name} & Name for the new test suite (non-\/\-N\-U\-L\-L). \\
\hline
{\em p\-Init} & Initialization function to call before running suite. \\
\hline
{\em p\-Clean} & Cleanup function to call after running suite. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Renvoie}
A pointer to the newly-\/created suite (N\-U\-L\-L if creation failed) 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\hypertarget{group__Framework_gad9f198a8a5fa8cc6870c3c8be873869f}{\index{Framework@{Framework}!C\-U\-\_\-add\-\_\-test@{C\-U\-\_\-add\-\_\-test}}
\index{C\-U\-\_\-add\-\_\-test@{C\-U\-\_\-add\-\_\-test}!Framework@{Framework}}
\subsubsection[{C\-U\-\_\-add\-\_\-test}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}C\-U\-\_\-\-E\-X\-P\-O\-R\-T {\bf C\-U\-\_\-p\-Test} C\-U\-\_\-add\-\_\-test (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf C\-U\-\_\-p\-Suite}}]{p\-Suite, }
\item[{const char $\ast$}]{str\-Name, }
\item[{{\bf C\-U\-\_\-\-Test\-Func}}]{p\-Test\-Func}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{group__Framework_gad9f198a8a5fa8cc6870c3c8be873869f}


This function creates a new test having the specified name and function, and adds it to the specified suite. 

The new test is active and able to be executed during a test run. At present, there is no mechanism for creating a test case independent of a suite. Neither p\-Suite, str\-Name, nor p\-Test\-Func may be N\-U\-L\-L.

The return value is a pointer to the newly-\/created test, or N\-U\-L\-L if there was a problem with the test creation or addition. An error code is also set for the framework. Note that if the name specified for the new test is a duplicate within p\-Suite, the test will be created and added but the error code will be set to C\-U\-E\-\_\-\-D\-U\-P\-\_\-\-T\-E\-S\-T. The duplicate test will not be accessible by name.\par
\par


N\-O\-T\-E -\/ the C\-U\-\_\-p\-Test pointer returned should N\-O\-T B\-E F\-R\-E\-E\-D B\-Y T\-H\-E U\-S\-E\-R. The test is freed by the C\-Unit system when \hyperlink{group__Framework_ga183eb7d7f79e149c767237cfef52cb82}{C\-U\-\_\-cleanup\-\_\-registry()} is called. {\bfseries This function must not be called during a test run (checked by assertion)}. \par
\par


\hyperlink{group__Framework_gad9f198a8a5fa8cc6870c3c8be873869f}{C\-U\-\_\-add\-\_\-test()} sets the following error codes\-:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item C\-U\-E\-\_\-\-S\-U\-C\-C\-E\-S\-S if no errors occurred.
\item C\-U\-E\-\_\-\-N\-O\-R\-E\-G\-I\-S\-T\-R\-Y if the registry has not been initialized.
\item C\-U\-E\-\_\-\-N\-O\-S\-U\-I\-T\-E if p\-Suite is N\-U\-L\-L.
\item C\-U\-E\-\_\-\-N\-O\-\_\-\-T\-E\-S\-T\-N\-A\-M\-E if str\-Name is N\-U\-L\-L.
\item C\-U\-E\-\_\-\-N\-O\-T\-E\-S\-T if p\-Test\-Func is N\-U\-L\-L.
\item C\-U\-E\-\_\-\-D\-U\-P\-\_\-\-T\-E\-S\-T if a test having str\-Name is already registered to p\-Suite.
\item C\-U\-E\-\_\-\-N\-O\-M\-E\-M\-O\-R\-Y if a memory allocation failed.\par
\par

\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Paramètres}
{\em p\-Suite} & Test suite to which to add new test (non-\/\-N\-U\-L\-L). \\
\hline
{\em str\-Name} & Name for the new test case (non-\/\-N\-U\-L\-L). \\
\hline
{\em p\-Test} & Function to call when running the test (non-\/\-N\-U\-L\-L). \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Renvoie}
A pointer to the newly-\/created test (N\-U\-L\-L if creation failed) 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\hypertarget{group__Framework_ga31a858e8b496b2af992b63902064c5fa}{\index{Framework@{Framework}!C\-U\-\_\-assert\-Implementation@{C\-U\-\_\-assert\-Implementation}}
\index{C\-U\-\_\-assert\-Implementation@{C\-U\-\_\-assert\-Implementation}!Framework@{Framework}}
\subsubsection[{C\-U\-\_\-assert\-Implementation}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}C\-U\-\_\-\-E\-X\-P\-O\-R\-T {\bf C\-U\-\_\-\-B\-O\-O\-L} C\-U\-\_\-assert\-Implementation (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf C\-U\-\_\-\-B\-O\-O\-L}}]{b\-Value, }
\item[{unsigned int}]{ui\-Line, }
\item[{const char $\ast$}]{str\-Condition, }
\item[{const char $\ast$}]{str\-File, }
\item[{const char $\ast$}]{str\-Function, }
\item[{{\bf C\-U\-\_\-\-B\-O\-O\-L}}]{b\-Fatal}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{group__Framework_ga31a858e8b496b2af992b63902064c5fa}


Assertion implementation function. 

All C\-Unit assertions reduce to a call to this function. It should only be called during an active test run (checked by assertion). This means that C\-Unit assertions should only be used in registered test functions during a test run.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Paramètres}
{\em b\-Value} & Value of the assertion (C\-U\-\_\-\-T\-R\-U\-E or C\-U\-\_\-\-F\-A\-L\-S\-E). \\
\hline
{\em ui\-Line} & Line number of failed test statement. \\
\hline
{\em str\-Condition} & String containing logical test that failed. \\
\hline
{\em str\-File} & Source file where test statement failed. \\
\hline
{\em str\-Function} & Function where test statement failed. \\
\hline
{\em b\-Fatal} & C\-U\-\_\-\-T\-R\-U\-E to abort test (via longjmp()), C\-U\-\_\-\-F\-A\-L\-S\-E to continue test. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Renvoie}
As a convenience, returns the value of the assertion (i.\-e. b\-Value). 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\hypertarget{group__Framework_ga183eb7d7f79e149c767237cfef52cb82}{\index{Framework@{Framework}!C\-U\-\_\-cleanup\-\_\-registry@{C\-U\-\_\-cleanup\-\_\-registry}}
\index{C\-U\-\_\-cleanup\-\_\-registry@{C\-U\-\_\-cleanup\-\_\-registry}!Framework@{Framework}}
\subsubsection[{C\-U\-\_\-cleanup\-\_\-registry}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}C\-U\-\_\-\-E\-X\-P\-O\-R\-T void C\-U\-\_\-cleanup\-\_\-registry (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{void}]{}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{group__Framework_ga183eb7d7f79e149c767237cfef52cb82}


Clears the test registry. 

The active test registry is freed, including all stored suites and associated tests. The most recent stored test results are also cleared. After calling this function, C\-Unit suites cannot be added until \hyperlink{group__Framework_ga3477b2d3e57c8f8aba36bbbdfa54920d}{C\-U\-\_\-initialize\-\_\-registry()} or \hyperlink{group__Framework_gaaec6d8893d61bfff165775385851562d}{C\-U\-\_\-set\-\_\-registry()} is called. Further, any pointers to suites or test cases held by the user will be invalidated by calling this function.\par
\par


This function may be called multiple times without generating an error condition. However, {\bfseries this function must not be called during a test run (checked by assertion)}

.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{Voir également}
\hyperlink{group__Framework_ga3477b2d3e57c8f8aba36bbbdfa54920d}{C\-U\-\_\-initialize\-\_\-registry}

\hyperlink{group__Framework_gaaec6d8893d61bfff165775385851562d}{C\-U\-\_\-set\-\_\-registry} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

Initializes the run summary information stored from the previous test run. 

Resets the run counts to zero, and frees any memory associated with failure records. Calling this function multiple times, while inefficient, will not cause an error condition. \begin{DoxySeeAlso}{Voir également}

\hypertarget{group__Framework_ga5d2ce564b228122842f515cb4e5beda2}{\index{Framework@{Framework}!C\-U\-\_\-create\-\_\-new\-\_\-registry@{C\-U\-\_\-create\-\_\-new\-\_\-registry}}

\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{void}]{}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{group__Framework_ga5d2ce564b228122842f515cb4e5beda2}


Creates and initializes a new test registry. 

Returns a pointer to a new, initialized registry (N\-U\-L\-L if memory could not be allocated). It is the caller's responsibility to destroy and free the new registry (unless it is made the active test registry using \hyperlink{group__Framework_gaaec6d8893d61bfff165775385851562d}{C\-U\-\_\-set\-\_\-registry()}). \hypertarget{group__Framework_ga7c46b0ae888482411575c93d5d780b0d}{\index{Framework@{Framework}!C\-U\-\_\-destroy\-\_\-existing\-\_\-registry@{C\-U\-\_\-destroy\-\_\-existing\-\_\-registry}}
\index{C\-U\-\_\-destroy\-\_\-existing\-\_\-registry@{C\-U\-\_\-destroy\-\_\-existing\-\_\-registry}!Framework@{Framework}}
\subsubsection[{C\-U\-\_\-destroy\-\_\-existing\-\_\-registry}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}C\-U\-\_\-\-E\-X\-P\-O\-R\-T void C\-U\-\_\-destroy\-\_\-existing\-\_\-registry (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf C\-U\-\_\-p\-Test\-Registry} $\ast$}]{pp\-Registry}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{group__Framework_ga7c46b0ae888482411575c93d5d780b0d}


Destroys and frees all memory for an existing test registry. 

The active test registry is destroyed by the C\-Unit system in \hyperlink{group__Framework_ga183eb7d7f79e149c767237cfef52cb82}{C\-U\-\_\-cleanup\-\_\-registry()}, so only call this function on registries created or held independently of the internal C\-Unit system.\par
\par


Once a registry is made the active test registry using \hyperlink{group__Framework_gaaec6d8893d61bfff165775385851562d}{C\-U\-\_\-set\-\_\-registry()}, its destruction will be handled by the framework. pp\-Registry may not be N\-U\-L\-L (checked by assertion), but $\ast$pp\-Registry can be N\-U\-L\-L (in which case the function has no effect). Note that $\ast$pp\-Registry will be set to N\-U\-L\-L on return.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Paramètres}
{\em pp\-Registry} & Address of a pointer to the registry to destroy (non-\/\-N\-U\-L\-L). \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

Retrieves the elapsed time for the last run in seconds (reset each run). 

This function will calculate the current elapsed time if the test run has not yet completed. This is in contrast to the run summary returned by \hyperlink{group__Framework_gad51994a28ffa19ba06b6c803d2796d94}{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-run\-\_\-summary()}, for which the elapsed time is not updated until the end of the run. \hypertarget{group__Framework_ga0bf3f9733e5fa0c0ed6ca0a37a2d995e}{\index{Framework@{Framework}!C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-error@{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-error}}

\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{void}]{}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{group__Framework_ga0bf3f9733e5fa0c0ed6ca0a37a2d995e}


Retrieves the current C\-Unit framework error code. 

C\-Unit implementation functions set the error code to indicate the status of the most recent operation. In general, the C\-Unit functions will clear the code to C\-U\-E\-\_\-\-S\-U\-C\-C\-E\-S\-S, then reset it to a specific error code if an exception condition is encountered. Some functions return the code, others leave it to the user to inspect if desired.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Renvoie}
The current error condition code. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

Retrieves a message corresponding to the current framework error code. 

C\-Unit implementation functions set the error code to indicate the of the most recent operation. In general, the C\-Unit functions will clear the code to C\-U\-E\-\_\-\-S\-U\-C\-C\-E\-S\-S, then reset it to a specific error code if an exception condition is encountered. This function allows the user to retrieve a descriptive error message corresponding to the error code set by the last operation.

\hypertarget{group__Framework_ga29e70990caa96ba6570bd6503650c4e7}{\index{Framework@{Framework}!C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-failure\-\_\-list@{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-failure\-\_\-list}}

)}}\label{group__Framework_ga29e70990caa96ba6570bd6503650c4e7}


Retrieves the head of the linked list of failures which occurred during the last run (reset each run). 

Note that the pointer returned is invalidated when the client initiates a run using \hyperlink{group__Framework_gada41915e7f9ae386ecc1bed20a79300b}{C\-U\-\_\-run\-\_\-all\-\_\-tests()}, \hyperlink{group__Framework_ga765ad6b90ec25090288ec10d34fc15c0}{C\-U\-\_\-run\-\_\-suite()}, or \hyperlink{group__Framework_ga4469c032ef93be8169d4869b22ceabd1}{C\-U\-\_\-run\-\_\-test()}. \hypertarget{group__Framework_ga2ac4bd2bd80e94b1288a472b12ee9931}{\index{Framework@{Framework}!C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-number\-\_\-of\-\_\-asserts@{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-number\-\_\-of\-\_\-asserts}}

\hypertarget{group__Framework_gacdc4bab7b0492ed1e3a4e076677de22e}{\index{Framework@{Framework}!C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-registry@{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-registry}}

\subsubsection[{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-registry}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}C\-U\-\_\-\-E\-X\-P\-O\-R\-T {\bf C\-U\-\_\-p\-Test\-Registry} C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-registry (

\item[{void}]{}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{group__Framework_gacdc4bab7b0492ed1e3a4e076677de22e}


Retrieves a pointer to the current test registry. 

Returns N\-U\-L\-L if the registry has not been initialized using \hyperlink{group__Framework_ga3477b2d3e57c8f8aba36bbbdfa54920d}{C\-U\-\_\-initialize\-\_\-registry()}. Directly accessing the registry should not be necessary for most users. This function is provided primarily for internal and testing purposes.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Renvoie}

\end{DoxyReturn}

\hyperlink{group__Framework_gaaec6d8893d61bfff165775385851562d}{C\-U\-\_\-set\-\_\-registry} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\hypertarget{group__Framework_ga829a4792d9de45459cc9e874f240ca5b}{\index{Framework@{Framework}!C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-run\-\_\-results\-\_\-string@{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-run\-\_\-results\-\_\-string}}
\index{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-run\-\_\-results\-\_\-string@{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-run\-\_\-results\-\_\-string}!Framework@{Framework}}
\subsubsection[{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-run\-\_\-results\-\_\-string}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}C\-U\-\_\-\-E\-X\-P\-O\-R\-T char$\ast$ C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-run\-\_\-results\-\_\-string (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{void}]{}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{group__Framework_ga829a4792d9de45459cc9e874f240ca5b}


Creates a string and fills it with a summary of the current run results. 

The run summary presents data for the suites, tests, and assertions encountered during the run, as well as the elapsed time. The data presented include the number of registered, run, passed, failed, and inactive entities for each, as well as the elapsed time. This function can be called at any time, although the test registry must have been initialized (checked by assertion). The returned string is owned by the caller and should be deallocated using \hyperlink{group__Framework_ga24a922b67c81baa3d7821fb425e094f4}{C\-U\-\_\-\-F\-R\-E\-E()}. N\-U\-L\-L is returned if there is an error allocating the new string.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Renvoie}
A new string containing the run summary (owned by caller). 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\hypertarget{group__Framework_gad51994a28ffa19ba06b6c803d2796d94}{\index{Framework@{Framework}!C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-run\-\_\-summary@{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-run\-\_\-summary}}
\index{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-run\-\_\-summary@{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-run\-\_\-summary}!Framework@{Framework}}
\subsubsection[{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-run\-\_\-summary}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}C\-U\-\_\-\-E\-X\-P\-O\-R\-T {\bf C\-U\-\_\-p\-Run\-Summary} C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-run\-\_\-summary (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{void}]{}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{group__Framework_gad51994a28ffa19ba06b6c803d2796d94}


Retrieves the entire run summary for the last test run (reset each run). 

The run counts and stats contained in the run summary are updated throughout a test run. Note, however, that the elapsed time is not updated until after all suites/tests are run but before the \char`\"{}all tests 
complete\char`\"{} message handler is called (if any). To get the elapsed time during a test run, use \hyperlink{group__Framework_ga80bc7ff46505762ac47c0997be1a32a4}{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-elapsed\-\_\-time()} instead. \hypertarget{group__Framework_ga58e560d695d4f6fdec8f2f2c9805bfcd}{\index{Framework@{Framework}!C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-suite@{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-suite}}
\index{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-suite@{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-suite}!Framework@{Framework}}
\subsubsection[{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-suite}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}C\-U\-\_\-\-E\-X\-P\-O\-R\-T {\bf C\-U\-\_\-p\-Suite} C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-suite (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{const char $\ast$}]{str\-Name}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{group__Framework_ga58e560d695d4f6fdec8f2f2c9805bfcd}


Retrieves the suite having the specified name. 

Searches the active test registry and returns a pointer to the 1st suite found. N\-U\-L\-L is returned if no suite having the specified name is found. In addition, the framework error state is set to C\-U\-E\-\_\-\-N\-O\-R\-E\-G\-I\-S\-T\-R\-Y if the registry is not initialized or to C\-U\-E\-\_\-\-N\-O\-\_\-\-S\-U\-I\-T\-E\-N\-A\-M\-E if str\-Name is N\-U\-L\-L. If the return value is N\-U\-L\-L and framework error state is C\-U\-E\-\_\-\-S\-U\-C\-C\-E\-S\-S, then the search simply failed to find the specified name. Use \hyperlink{group__Framework_ga66cbc0f181722251ac52a28eb26e7886}{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-suite\-\_\-at\-\_\-pos()} to retrieve a suite by position rather than name.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Paramètres}
{\em str\-Name} & The name of the suite to search for (non-\/\-N\-U\-L\-L). \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Renvoie}
Returns a pointer to the suite, or N\-U\-L\-L if not found or an error occurred. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{Voir également}
\hyperlink{group__Framework_ga66cbc0f181722251ac52a28eb26e7886}{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-suite\-\_\-at\-\_\-pos()} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\hypertarget{group__Framework_ga66cbc0f181722251ac52a28eb26e7886}{\index{Framework@{Framework}!C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-suite\-\_\-at\-\_\-pos@{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-suite\-\_\-at\-\_\-pos}}
\index{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-suite\-\_\-at\-\_\-pos@{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-suite\-\_\-at\-\_\-pos}!Framework@{Framework}}
\subsubsection[{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-suite\-\_\-at\-\_\-pos}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}C\-U\-\_\-\-E\-X\-P\-O\-R\-T {\bf C\-U\-\_\-p\-Suite} C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-suite\-\_\-at\-\_\-pos (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{unsigned int}]{pos}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{group__Framework_ga66cbc0f181722251ac52a28eb26e7886}


Retrieves the suite at the specified position. 

Iterates the active test registry and returns a pointer to the suite at position pos. pos is a 1-\/based index having valid values \mbox{[}1 .. \hyperlink{group__Framework_gacdc4bab7b0492ed1e3a4e076677de22e}{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-registry()}-\/$>$ui\-Number\-Of\-Suites\mbox{]} and corresponds to the order in which suites were registered. If pos is invalid or an error occurs, 0 is returned. In addition, the framework error state is set to C\-U\-E\-\_\-\-N\-O\-R\-E\-G\-I\-S\-T\-R\-Y if the registry is not initialized, or C\-U\-E\-\_\-\-S\-U\-C\-C\-E\-S\-S if pos was invalid. Use \hyperlink{group__Framework_ga58e560d695d4f6fdec8f2f2c9805bfcd}{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-suite()} to retrieve a suite by name rather than position.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Paramètres}
{\em pos} & The 1-\/based position of the suite to fetch. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Renvoie}
Returns a pointer to the suite, or 0 if not found or an error occurred. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{Voir également}
\hyperlink{group__Framework_ga58e560d695d4f6fdec8f2f2c9805bfcd}{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-suite()} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\hypertarget{group__Framework_ga75a31876ad11c8e5a6a5fadea7ef1051}{\index{Framework@{Framework}!C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-suite\-\_\-by\-\_\-index@{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-suite\-\_\-by\-\_\-index}}
\index{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-suite\-\_\-by\-\_\-index@{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-suite\-\_\-by\-\_\-index}!Framework@{Framework}}
\subsubsection[{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-suite\-\_\-by\-\_\-index}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}C\-U\-\_\-\-E\-X\-P\-O\-R\-T {\bf C\-U\-\_\-p\-Suite} C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-suite\-\_\-by\-\_\-index (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}

\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{group__Framework_ga75a31876ad11c8e5a6a5fadea7ef1051}


Retrieves a pointer to the suite at the specified (1-\/based) index. 

Iterates p\-Registry and returns a pointer to the suite located at the specified index. p\-Registry may not be N\-U\-L\-L (checked by assertion). Clients should normally use \hyperlink{group__Framework_ga66cbc0f181722251ac52a28eb26e7886}{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-suite\-\_\-at\-\_\-pos()} instead, which automatically searches the active test registry.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Paramètres}
{\em index} & The 1-\/based index of the suite to find. \\
\hline
{\em p\-Registry} & The registry to scan (non-\/\-N\-U\-L\-L). \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Renvoie}
Pointer to the suite at the specified index, or N\-U\-L\-L if index is invalid. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{Voir également}
\hyperlink{group__Framework_ga66cbc0f181722251ac52a28eb26e7886}{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-suite\-\_\-at\-\_\-pos()} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\hypertarget{group__Framework_ga625d2e3767cdb663399a99cf88321e60}{\index{Framework@{Framework}!C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-suite\-\_\-by\-\_\-name@{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-suite\-\_\-by\-\_\-name}}
\index{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-suite\-\_\-by\-\_\-name@{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-suite\-\_\-by\-\_\-name}!Framework@{Framework}}
\subsubsection[{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-suite\-\_\-by\-\_\-name}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}C\-U\-\_\-\-E\-X\-P\-O\-R\-T {\bf C\-U\-\_\-p\-Suite} C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-suite\-\_\-by\-\_\-name (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{const char $\ast$}]{sz\-Suite\-Name, }
\item[{{\bf C\-U\-\_\-p\-Test\-Registry}}]{p\-Registry}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{group__Framework_ga625d2e3767cdb663399a99cf88321e60}


Retrieves a pointer to the suite having the specified name. 

Scans the p\-Registry and returns a pointer to the first suite located having the specified name. Neither sz\-Suite\-Name nor p\-Registry may be N\-U\-L\-L (checked by assertion). Clients should normally use \hyperlink{group__Framework_ga58e560d695d4f6fdec8f2f2c9805bfcd}{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-suite()} instead, which automatically searches the active test registry.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Paramètres}
{\em sz\-Suite\-Name} & The name of the suite to locate (non-\/\-N\-U\-L\-L). \\
\hline
{\em p\-Registry} & The registry to scan (non-\/\-N\-U\-L\-L). \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Renvoie}
Pointer to the first suite having the specified name, N\-U\-L\-L if not found. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{Voir également}
\hyperlink{group__Framework_ga58e560d695d4f6fdec8f2f2c9805bfcd}{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-suite()} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\hypertarget{group__Framework_ga9d180e4db3591109077c81c6ab4cb151}{\index{Framework@{Framework}!C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-suite\-\_\-cleanup\-\_\-failure\-\_\-handler@{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-suite\-\_\-cleanup\-\_\-failure\-\_\-handler}}
\index{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-suite\-\_\-cleanup\-\_\-failure\-\_\-handler@{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-suite\-\_\-cleanup\-\_\-failure\-\_\-handler}!Framework@{Framework}}
\subsubsection[{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-suite\-\_\-cleanup\-\_\-failure\-\_\-handler}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}C\-U\-\_\-\-E\-X\-P\-O\-R\-T {\bf C\-U\-\_\-\-Suite\-Cleanup\-Failure\-Message\-Handler} C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-suite\-\_\-cleanup\-\_\-failure\-\_\-handler (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{void}]{}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{group__Framework_ga9d180e4db3591109077c81c6ab4cb151}


Retrieves the message handler called when a suite cleanup error occurs.

\hypertarget{group__Framework_ga49a20837af93245aa578935758c7810c}{\index{Framework@{Framework}!C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-suite\-\_\-pos@{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-suite\-\_\-pos}}
\index{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-suite\-\_\-pos@{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-suite\-\_\-pos}!Framework@{Framework}}
\subsubsection[{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-suite\-\_\-pos}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}C\-U\-\_\-\-E\-X\-P\-O\-R\-T unsigned int C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-suite\-\_\-pos (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf C\-U\-\_\-p\-Suite}}]{p\-Suite}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{group__Framework_ga49a20837af93245aa578935758c7810c}


Looks up the position of the specified suite. 

The position is a 1-\/based index of suites in the active test registry which corresponds to the order in which suites were registered. If p\-Suite is not found or an error occurs, 0 is returned. In addition, the framework error state is set to C\-U\-E\-\_\-\-N\-O\-R\-E\-G\-I\-S\-T\-R\-Y if the registry is not initialized, or C\-U\-E\-\_\-\-N\-O\-S\-U\-I\-T\-E if p\-Suite is N\-U\-L\-L. The returned position may be used to retrieve the suite using C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-suite\-\_\-by\-\_\-pos().


\begin{DoxyParams}{Paramètres}
{\em p\-Suite} & Pointer to the suite to find (non-\/\-N\-U\-L\-L). \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Renvoie}
Returns the 1-\/based position of p\-Suite in the registry, or N\-U\-L\-L if not found or an error occurred. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{Voir également}
C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-suite\-\_\-by\-\_\-pos() 

\hyperlink{group__Framework_gab8f529d5919f590593210eb2dcec37f1}{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-suite\-\_\-pos\-\_\-by\-\_\-name()} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\hypertarget{group__Framework_gab8f529d5919f590593210eb2dcec37f1}{\index{Framework@{Framework}!C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-suite\-\_\-pos\-\_\-by\-\_\-name@{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-suite\-\_\-pos\-\_\-by\-\_\-name}}
\index{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-suite\-\_\-pos\-\_\-by\-\_\-name@{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-suite\-\_\-pos\-\_\-by\-\_\-name}!Framework@{Framework}}
\subsubsection[{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-suite\-\_\-pos\-\_\-by\-\_\-name}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}C\-U\-\_\-\-E\-X\-P\-O\-R\-T unsigned int C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-suite\-\_\-pos\-\_\-by\-\_\-name (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{const char $\ast$}]{str\-Name}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{group__Framework_gab8f529d5919f590593210eb2dcec37f1}


Looks up the position of the suite having the specified name. 

The position is a 1-\/based index of suites in the active test registry which corresponds to the order in which suites were registered. If no suite has the specified name or an error occurs, 0 is returned. In addition, the framework error state is set to C\-U\-E\-\_\-\-N\-O\-R\-E\-G\-I\-S\-T\-R\-Y if the registry is not initialized, or C\-U\-E\-\_\-\-N\-O\-\_\-\-S\-U\-I\-T\-E\-N\-A\-M\-E if str\-Name is N\-U\-L\-L. The search ends at the 1st suite found having name str\-Name. The returned position may be used to retrieve the suite using C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-suite\-\_\-by\-\_\-pos().


\begin{DoxyParams}{Paramètres}
{\em str\-Name} & Name of the suite to find (non-\/\-N\-U\-L\-L). \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Renvoie}
Returns the 1-\/based position of p\-Suite in the registry, or N\-U\-L\-L if not found or an error occurred. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{Voir également}

\hyperlink{group__Framework_gab8f529d5919f590593210eb2dcec37f1}{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-suite\-\_\-pos\-\_\-by\-\_\-name()}

\hypertarget{group__Framework_ga4403d186236201362d04069c9565a777}{\index{Framework@{Framework}!C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-suite\-\_\-start\-\_\-handler@{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-suite\-\_\-start\-\_\-handler}}

\hypertarget{group__Framework_ga032d257cade342d583d56a1346222d12}{\index{Framework@{Framework}!C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-test@{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-test}}
\index{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-test@{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-test}!Framework@{Framework}}
\subsubsection[{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-test}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}C\-U\-\_\-\-E\-X\-P\-O\-R\-T {\bf C\-U\-\_\-p\-Test} C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-test (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf C\-U\-\_\-p\-Suite}}]{p\-Suite, }
\item[{const char $\ast$}]{str\-Name}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{group__Framework_ga032d257cade342d583d56a1346222d12}


Retrieves the test having the specified name. 

Searches p\-Suite and returns a pointer to the 1st test found named str\-Name. N\-U\-L\-L is returned if no test having the specified name is found in p\-Suite. In addition, the framework error state is set as follows\-:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item C\-U\-E\-\_\-\-N\-O\-R\-E\-G\-I\-S\-T\-R\-Y if the registry is not initialized
\item C\-U\-E\-\_\-\-N\-O\-S\-U\-I\-T\-E if p\-Suite is N\-U\-L\-L
\item C\-U\-E\-\_\-\-N\-O\-\_\-\-T\-E\-S\-T\-N\-A\-M\-E if str\-Name is N\-U\-L\-L.
\end{DoxyItemize}

If the return value is N\-U\-L\-L and framework error state is C\-U\-E\-\_\-\-S\-U\-C\-C\-E\-S\-S, then the search simply failed to find the specified name. Use \hyperlink{group__Framework_ga75d44f091f3ab0ec818fa0edfec0d465}{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-test\-\_\-at\-\_\-pos()} to retrieve a test by position rather than name.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Paramètres}
{\em p\-Suite} & Pointer to the suite to search (non-\/\-N\-U\-L\-L). \\
\hline
{\em str\-Name} & The name of the test to search for (non-\/\-N\-U\-L\-L). \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Renvoie}
Returns a pointer to the test, or N\-U\-L\-L if not found or an error occurred. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{Voir également}
\hyperlink{group__Framework_ga75d44f091f3ab0ec818fa0edfec0d465}{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-test\-\_\-at\-\_\-pos()} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\hypertarget{group__Framework_ga75d44f091f3ab0ec818fa0edfec0d465}{\index{Framework@{Framework}!C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-test\-\_\-at\-\_\-pos@{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-test\-\_\-at\-\_\-pos}}
\index{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-test\-\_\-at\-\_\-pos@{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-test\-\_\-at\-\_\-pos}!Framework@{Framework}}
\subsubsection[{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-test\-\_\-at\-\_\-pos}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}C\-U\-\_\-\-E\-X\-P\-O\-R\-T {\bf C\-U\-\_\-p\-Test} C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-test\-\_\-at\-\_\-pos (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf C\-U\-\_\-p\-Suite}}]{p\-Suite, }
\item[{unsigned int}]{pos}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{group__Framework_ga75d44f091f3ab0ec818fa0edfec0d465}


Retrieves the test at the specified position in p\-Suite. 

Iterates the tests registered in p\-Suite and returns a pointer to the test at position pos. pos is a 1-\/based index having valid values \mbox{[}1 .. p\-Suite-\/$>$ui\-Number\-Of\-Tests\mbox{]} and corresponds to the order in which tests were added to p\-Suite. If pos is invalid or an error occurs, 0 is returned. In addition, the framework error state is set as follows\-:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item C\-U\-E\-\_\-\-N\-O\-R\-E\-G\-I\-S\-T\-R\-Y if the registry is not initialized
\item C\-U\-E\-\_\-\-N\-O\-S\-U\-I\-T\-E if p\-Suite is N\-U\-L\-L Use \hyperlink{group__Framework_ga032d257cade342d583d56a1346222d12}{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-test()} to retrieve a test by name rather than position.
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Paramètres}
{\em p\-Suite} & Pointer to the suite to search (non-\/\-N\-U\-L\-L). \\
\hline
{\em pos} & The 1-\/based position of the test to fetch. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Renvoie}
Returns a pointer to the test, or 0 if not found or an error occurred. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{Voir également}
\hyperlink{group__Framework_ga032d257cade342d583d56a1346222d12}{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-test()} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\hypertarget{group__Framework_gad12cd874661530cd3aa61d715be58dd6}{\index{Framework@{Framework}!C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-test\-\_\-by\-\_\-index@{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-test\-\_\-by\-\_\-index}}
\index{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-test\-\_\-by\-\_\-index@{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-test\-\_\-by\-\_\-index}!Framework@{Framework}}
\subsubsection[{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-test\-\_\-by\-\_\-index}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}C\-U\-\_\-\-E\-X\-P\-O\-R\-T {\bf C\-U\-\_\-p\-Test} C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-test\-\_\-by\-\_\-index (

\item[{{\bf C\-U\-\_\-p\-Suite}}]{p\-Suite}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{group__Framework_gad12cd874661530cd3aa61d715be58dd6}


Retrieves a pointer to the test at the specified (1-\/based) index. 

Iterates p\-Suite and returns a pointer to the test located at the specified index. p\-Suite may not be N\-U\-L\-L (checked by assertion). Clients should normally use \hyperlink{group__Framework_ga75d44f091f3ab0ec818fa0edfec0d465}{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-test\-\_\-at\-\_\-pos()} instead, which automatically searches the active test registry.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Paramètres}
{\em index} & The 1-\/based index of the test to find. \\
\hline
{\em p\-Registry} & The registry to scan (non-\/\-N\-U\-L\-L). \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Renvoie}
Pointer to the test at the specified index, or N\-U\-L\-L if index is invalid. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{Voir également}
\hyperlink{group__Framework_ga75d44f091f3ab0ec818fa0edfec0d465}{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-test\-\_\-at\-\_\-pos()} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\hypertarget{group__Framework_gab627141bbc9dff09228530d289517e9c}{\index{Framework@{Framework}!C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-test\-\_\-by\-\_\-name@{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-test\-\_\-by\-\_\-name}}

\subsubsection[{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-test\-\_\-by\-\_\-name}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}C\-U\-\_\-\-E\-X\-P\-O\-R\-T {\bf C\-U\-\_\-p\-Test} C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-test\-\_\-by\-\_\-name (

)}}\label{group__Framework_gab627141bbc9dff09228530d289517e9c}


Retrieves a pointer to the test case in p\-Suite having the specified name. 

The first test case in p\-Suite having the specified name is returned, or N\-U\-L\-L if not found. Neither sz\-Suite\-Name nor p\-Suite may be N\-U\-L\-L (checked by assertion). Clients should normally use \hyperlink{group__Framework_ga032d257cade342d583d56a1346222d12}{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-test()} instead.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Paramètres}

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Renvoie}

\end{DoxyReturn}

\hypertarget{group__Framework_ga30be88922ceec733a8aa7d44ed366170}{\index{Framework@{Framework}!C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-test\-\_\-pos@{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-test\-\_\-pos}}
\index{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-test\-\_\-pos@{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-test\-\_\-pos}!Framework@{Framework}}
\subsubsection[{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-test\-\_\-pos}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}C\-U\-\_\-\-E\-X\-P\-O\-R\-T unsigned int C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-test\-\_\-pos (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}

\item[{{\bf C\-U\-\_\-p\-Test}}]{p\-Test}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{group__Framework_ga30be88922ceec733a8aa7d44ed366170}


Looks up the position of the specified test in p\-Suite. 

The position is a 1-\/based index of tests in p\-Suite which corresponds to the order in which tests were added. If p\-Test is not found or an error occurs, 0 is returned. In addition, the framework error state is set as follows\-:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item C\-U\-E\-\_\-\-N\-O\-R\-E\-G\-I\-S\-T\-R\-Y if the registry is not initialized
\item C\-U\-E\-\_\-\-N\-O\-S\-U\-I\-T\-E if p\-Suite is N\-U\-L\-L
\item C\-U\-E\-\_\-\-N\-O\-T\-E\-S\-T if p\-Test is N\-U\-L\-L
\end{DoxyItemize}

The returned position may be used to retrieve the test using C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-test\-\_\-by\-\_\-pos().


\begin{DoxyParams}{Paramètres}
{\em p\-Suite} & Pointer to the suite to search (non-\/\-N\-U\-L\-L). \\
\hline
{\em p\-Test} & Pointer to the test to find (non-\/\-N\-U\-L\-L). \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Renvoie}
Returns the 1-\/based position of p\-Test in p\-Suite, or N\-U\-L\-L if not found or an error occurred. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

The position is a 1-\/based index of tests in p\-Suite which corresponds to the order in which tests were added. If no test has the specified name or an error occurs, 0 is returned. In addition, the framework error state is set as follows\-:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item C\-U\-E\-\_\-\-N\-O\-R\-E\-G\-I\-S\-T\-R\-Y if the registry is not initialized
\item C\-U\-E\-\_\-\-N\-O\-S\-U\-I\-T\-E if p\-Suite is N\-U\-L\-L
\item C\-U\-E\-\_\-\-N\-O\-\_\-\-T\-E\-S\-T\-N\-A\-M\-E if str\-Name is N\-U\-L\-L The search ends at the 1st test found having name str\-Name. The returned position may be used to retrieve the suite using C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-test\-\_\-by\-\_\-pos().

\hypertarget{group__Framework_gaa68ed834a6a3c4b1bfd5beaa9b40a735}{\index{Framework@{Framework}!C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-test\-\_\-start\-\_\-handler@{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-test\-\_\-start\-\_\-handler}}

\end{DoxyParamCaption}

\hypertarget{group__Framework_ga3477b2d3e57c8f8aba36bbbdfa54920d}{\index{Framework@{Framework}!C\-U\-\_\-initialize\-\_\-registry@{C\-U\-\_\-initialize\-\_\-registry}}
\index{C\-U\-\_\-initialize\-\_\-registry@{C\-U\-\_\-initialize\-\_\-registry}!Framework@{Framework}}
\subsubsection[{C\-U\-\_\-initialize\-\_\-registry}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}C\-U\-\_\-\-E\-X\-P\-O\-R\-T {\bf C\-U\-\_\-\-Error\-Code} C\-U\-\_\-initialize\-\_\-registry (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{void}]{}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{group__Framework_ga3477b2d3e57c8f8aba36bbbdfa54920d}


Initializes the framework test registry. 

Any existing registry is freed, including all stored suites and associated tests. It is not necessary to explicitly call \hyperlink{group__Framework_ga183eb7d7f79e149c767237cfef52cb82}{C\-U\-\_\-cleanup\-\_\-registry()} before reinitializing the framework. The most recent stored test results are also cleared.\par
\par


{\bfseries This function must not be called during a test run (checked by assertion)}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Renvoie}
C\-U\-E\-\_\-\-N\-O\-M\-E\-M\-O\-R\-Y if memory for the new registry cannot be allocated, C\-U\-E\-\_\-\-S\-U\-C\-C\-E\-S\-S otherwise. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\hypertarget{group__Framework_ga0eb46055f2b8a8ec90e3c24562e9b9fb}{\index{Framework@{Framework}!C\-U\-\_\-print\-\_\-run\-\_\-results@{C\-U\-\_\-print\-\_\-run\-\_\-results}}
\index{C\-U\-\_\-print\-\_\-run\-\_\-results@{C\-U\-\_\-print\-\_\-run\-\_\-results}!Framework@{Framework}}
\subsubsection[{C\-U\-\_\-print\-\_\-run\-\_\-results}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}C\-U\-\_\-\-E\-X\-P\-O\-R\-T void C\-U\-\_\-print\-\_\-run\-\_\-results (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{F\-I\-L\-E $\ast$}]{file}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{group__Framework_ga0eb46055f2b8a8ec90e3c24562e9b9fb}


Prints a summary of the current run results to file. 

The run summary is the same as returned by \hyperlink{group__Framework_ga829a4792d9de45459cc9e874f240ca5b}{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-run\-\_\-results\-\_\-string()}. Note that no newlines are printed before or after the report, so any positioning must be performed before/after calling this function. The report itself extends over several lines broken by '\par
' characters. file may not be N\-U\-L\-L (checked by assertion).


\begin{DoxyParams}{Paramètres}
{\em file} & Pointer to stream to receive the printed summary (non-\/\-N\-U\-L\-L). \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\hypertarget{group__Framework_gaef02c65058bfe9f3adc320d536428588}{\index{Framework@{Framework}!C\-U\-\_\-register\-\_\-nsuites@{C\-U\-\_\-register\-\_\-nsuites}}
\index{C\-U\-\_\-register\-\_\-nsuites@{C\-U\-\_\-register\-\_\-nsuites}!Framework@{Framework}}
\subsubsection[{C\-U\-\_\-register\-\_\-nsuites}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}C\-U\-\_\-\-E\-X\-P\-O\-R\-T {\bf C\-U\-\_\-\-Error\-Code} C\-U\-\_\-register\-\_\-nsuites (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{int}]{suite\-\_\-count, }
\item[{}]{...}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{group__Framework_gaef02c65058bfe9f3adc320d536428588}


Registers multiple suite arrays in \hyperlink{structCU__SuiteInfo}{C\-U\-\_\-\-Suite\-Info} format. 

The function accepts a variable number of suite arrays to be registered. The number of arrays is indicated by the value of the 1st argument, suite\-\_\-count. Each suite in each array is registered with the C\-Unit test registry, along with all of the associated tests.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Paramètres}
{\em suite\-\_\-count} & The number of C\-U\-\_\-\-Suite\-Info$\ast$ arguments to follow. \\
\hline
{\em ...} & suite\-\_\-count number of C\-U\-\_\-\-Suite\-Info$\ast$ arguments. N\-U\-L\-Ls are ignored. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Renvoie}
A C\-U\-\_\-\-Error\-Code indicating the error status. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{Voir également}
\hyperlink{group__Framework_ga331001da0a8bd8faececdb48e7ad3f96}{C\-U\-\_\-register\-\_\-suites()} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\hypertarget{group__Framework_ga331001da0a8bd8faececdb48e7ad3f96}{\index{Framework@{Framework}!C\-U\-\_\-register\-\_\-suites@{C\-U\-\_\-register\-\_\-suites}}
\index{C\-U\-\_\-register\-\_\-suites@{C\-U\-\_\-register\-\_\-suites}!Framework@{Framework}}
\subsubsection[{C\-U\-\_\-register\-\_\-suites}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}C\-U\-\_\-\-E\-X\-P\-O\-R\-T {\bf C\-U\-\_\-\-Error\-Code} C\-U\-\_\-register\-\_\-suites (

Registers the suites in a single \hyperlink{structCU__SuiteInfo}{C\-U\-\_\-\-Suite\-Info} array. 

Multiple arrays can be registered using \hyperlink{group__Framework_gaef02c65058bfe9f3adc320d536428588}{C\-U\-\_\-register\-\_\-nsuites()}.

\hypertarget{group__Framework_gab976af96105872cb082ff4835cac1696}{\index{Framework@{Framework}!C\-U\-\_\-registry\-\_\-initialized@{C\-U\-\_\-registry\-\_\-initialized}}

\hyperlink{group__Framework_ga183eb7d7f79e149c767237cfef52cb82}{C\-U\-\_\-cleanup\-\_\-registry} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\hypertarget{group__Framework_gada41915e7f9ae386ecc1bed20a79300b}{\index{Framework@{Framework}!C\-U\-\_\-run\-\_\-all\-\_\-tests@{C\-U\-\_\-run\-\_\-all\-\_\-tests}}
\index{C\-U\-\_\-run\-\_\-all\-\_\-tests@{C\-U\-\_\-run\-\_\-all\-\_\-tests}!Framework@{Framework}}
\subsubsection[{C\-U\-\_\-run\-\_\-all\-\_\-tests}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}C\-U\-\_\-\-E\-X\-P\-O\-R\-T {\bf C\-U\-\_\-\-Error\-Code} C\-U\-\_\-run\-\_\-all\-\_\-tests (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{void}]{}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{group__Framework_gada41915e7f9ae386ecc1bed20a79300b}


Runs all tests in all suites registered in the test registry. 

The suites are run in the order registered in the test registry. For each suite, it is first checked to make sure it is active. Any initialization function is then called, the suite is run using run\-\_\-single\-\_\-suite(), and finally any suite cleanup function is called. If an error condition (other than C\-U\-E\-\_\-\-N\-O\-R\-E\-G\-I\-S\-T\-R\-Y) occurs during the run, the action depends on the current error action (see \hyperlink{group__Framework_ga58f4bdc1a05802f89005a487768b3d75}{C\-U\-\_\-set\-\_\-error\-\_\-action()}). An inactive suite is not considered an error for this function. Note that the run statistics (counts of tests, successes, failures) are cleared each time this function is run, even if it is unsuccessful.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Renvoie}
A C\-U\-\_\-\-Error\-Code indicating the first error condition encountered while running the tests. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{Voir également}
\hyperlink{group__Framework_ga765ad6b90ec25090288ec10d34fc15c0}{C\-U\-\_\-run\-\_\-suite()} to run the tests in a specific suite. 

\hyperlink{group__Framework_ga4469c032ef93be8169d4869b22ceabd1}{C\-U\-\_\-run\-\_\-test()} for run a specific test only. 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\hypertarget{group__Framework_ga765ad6b90ec25090288ec10d34fc15c0}{\index{Framework@{Framework}!C\-U\-\_\-run\-\_\-suite@{C\-U\-\_\-run\-\_\-suite}}
\index{C\-U\-\_\-run\-\_\-suite@{C\-U\-\_\-run\-\_\-suite}!Framework@{Framework}}
\subsubsection[{C\-U\-\_\-run\-\_\-suite}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}C\-U\-\_\-\-E\-X\-P\-O\-R\-T {\bf C\-U\-\_\-\-Error\-Code} C\-U\-\_\-run\-\_\-suite (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf C\-U\-\_\-p\-Suite}}]{p\-Suite}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{group__Framework_ga765ad6b90ec25090288ec10d34fc15c0}


Runs all tests in a specified suite. 

The suite need not be registered in the test registry to be run. It does, however, need to have its f\-Active flag set to C\-U\-\_\-\-T\-R\-U\-E.\par
\par


Any initialization function for the suite is first called, then the suite is run using run\-\_\-single\-\_\-suite(), and any suite cleanup function is called. Note that the run statistics (counts of tests, successes, failures) are initialized each time this function is called even if it is unsuccessful. If an error condition occurs during the run, the action depends on the current error action (see \hyperlink{group__Framework_ga58f4bdc1a05802f89005a487768b3d75}{C\-U\-\_\-set\-\_\-error\-\_\-action()}).


\begin{DoxyParams}{Paramètres}
{\em p\-Suite} & The suite containing the test (non-\/\-N\-U\-L\-L) \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Renvoie}
A C\-U\-\_\-\-Error\-Code indicating the first error condition encountered while running the suite. \hyperlink{group__Framework_ga765ad6b90ec25090288ec10d34fc15c0}{C\-U\-\_\-run\-\_\-suite()} sets and returns C\-U\-E\-\_\-\-N\-O\-S\-U\-I\-T\-E if p\-Suite is N\-U\-L\-L, or C\-U\-E\-\_\-\-S\-U\-I\-T\-E\-\_\-\-I\-N\-A\-C\-T\-I\-V\-E if the requested suite is not activated. Other error codes can be set during suite initialization or cleanup or during test runs. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{Voir également}
\hyperlink{group__Framework_gada41915e7f9ae386ecc1bed20a79300b}{C\-U\-\_\-run\-\_\-all\-\_\-tests()} to run all suites. 

\hyperlink{group__Framework_ga4469c032ef93be8169d4869b22ceabd1}{C\-U\-\_\-run\-\_\-test()} to run a single test in a specific suite. 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\hypertarget{group__Framework_ga4469c032ef93be8169d4869b22ceabd1}{\index{Framework@{Framework}!C\-U\-\_\-run\-\_\-test@{C\-U\-\_\-run\-\_\-test}}
\index{C\-U\-\_\-run\-\_\-test@{C\-U\-\_\-run\-\_\-test}!Framework@{Framework}}
\subsubsection[{C\-U\-\_\-run\-\_\-test}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}C\-U\-\_\-\-E\-X\-P\-O\-R\-T {\bf C\-U\-\_\-\-Error\-Code} C\-U\-\_\-run\-\_\-test (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf C\-U\-\_\-p\-Suite}}]{p\-Suite, }
\item[{{\bf C\-U\-\_\-p\-Test}}]{p\-Test}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{group__Framework_ga4469c032ef93be8169d4869b22ceabd1}


Runs a specific test in a specified suite. 

The suite need not be registered in the test registry to be run, although the test must be registered in the specified suite. Any initialization function for the suite is first called, then the test is run using run\-\_\-single\-\_\-test(), and any suite cleanup function is called. Note that the run statistics (counts of tests, successes, failures) will be initialized each time this function is called even if it is not successful. Both the suite and test specified must be active for the test to be run. The suite is not considered to be run, although it may be counted as a failed suite if the intialization or cleanup functions fail.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Paramètres}
{\em p\-Suite} & The suite containing the test (non-\/\-N\-U\-L\-L) \\
\hline
{\em p\-Test} & The test to run (non-\/\-N\-U\-L\-L) \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Renvoie}
A C\-U\-\_\-\-Error\-Code indicating the first error condition encountered while running the suite. \hyperlink{group__Framework_ga4469c032ef93be8169d4869b22ceabd1}{C\-U\-\_\-run\-\_\-test()} sets and returns C\-U\-E\-\_\-\-N\-O\-S\-U\-I\-T\-E if p\-Suite is N\-U\-L\-L, C\-U\-E\-\_\-\-N\-O\-T\-E\-S\-T if p\-Test is N\-U\-L\-L, C\-U\-E\-\_\-\-S\-U\-I\-T\-E\-\_\-\-I\-N\-A\-C\-T\-I\-V\-E if p\-Suite is not active, C\-U\-E\-\_\-\-T\-E\-S\-T\-\_\-\-N\-O\-T\-\_\-\-I\-N\-\_\-\-S\-U\-I\-T\-E if p\-Test is not registered in p\-Suite, and C\-U\-\_\-\-T\-E\-S\-T\-\_\-\-I\-N\-A\-C\-T\-I\-V\-E if p\-Test is not active. Other error codes can be set during suite initialization or cleanup or during the test run. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{Voir également}
\hyperlink{group__Framework_gada41915e7f9ae386ecc1bed20a79300b}{C\-U\-\_\-run\-\_\-all\-\_\-tests()} to run all tests/suites. 

\hyperlink{group__Framework_ga765ad6b90ec25090288ec10d34fc15c0}{C\-U\-\_\-run\-\_\-suite()} to run all tests in a specific suite. 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\hypertarget{group__Framework_ga875c98c7ec5df1a0450f1054a91506fb}{\index{Framework@{Framework}!C\-U\-\_\-set\-\_\-all\-\_\-test\-\_\-complete\-\_\-handler@{C\-U\-\_\-set\-\_\-all\-\_\-test\-\_\-complete\-\_\-handler}}
\index{C\-U\-\_\-set\-\_\-all\-\_\-test\-\_\-complete\-\_\-handler@{C\-U\-\_\-set\-\_\-all\-\_\-test\-\_\-complete\-\_\-handler}!Framework@{Framework}}
\subsubsection[{C\-U\-\_\-set\-\_\-all\-\_\-test\-\_\-complete\-\_\-handler}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}C\-U\-\_\-\-E\-X\-P\-O\-R\-T void C\-U\-\_\-set\-\_\-all\-\_\-test\-\_\-complete\-\_\-handler (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf C\-U\-\_\-\-All\-Tests\-Complete\-Message\-Handler}}]{p\-All\-Tests\-Complete\-Message}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{group__Framework_ga875c98c7ec5df1a0450f1054a91506fb}


Sets the message handler to call after all tests have been run. 

\hypertarget{group__Framework_ga2e817abf46a330a699fe5f472f5bfd64}{\index{Framework@{Framework}!C\-U\-\_\-set\-\_\-error@{C\-U\-\_\-set\-\_\-error}}
\index{C\-U\-\_\-set\-\_\-error@{C\-U\-\_\-set\-\_\-error}!Framework@{Framework}}
\subsubsection[{C\-U\-\_\-set\-\_\-error}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}C\-U\-\_\-\-E\-X\-P\-O\-R\-T void C\-U\-\_\-set\-\_\-error (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf C\-U\-\_\-\-Error\-Code}}]{error}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{group__Framework_ga2e817abf46a330a699fe5f472f5bfd64}


Sets the C\-Unit framework error code. 

This function is used internally by C\-Unit implementation functions when an error condition occurs within the framework. It should not generally be called by user code. N\-O\-T\-E that if the current error action is C\-U\-E\-A\-\_\-\-A\-B\-O\-R\-T, then calling this function will result in exit() being called for the current application.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Paramètres}
{\em error} & C\-U\-\_\-\-Error\-Code indicating the current error condition. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{Voir également}
\hyperlink{group__Framework_ga0bf3f9733e5fa0c0ed6ca0a37a2d995e}{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-error()} 

\hyperlink{group__Framework_gaee27bf496da77437288bc9fe2a0b20ed}{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-error\-\_\-msg()} 

\hyperlink{group__Framework_ga743a2a025ee3eb792d7d85f0eea347e6}{C\-U\-\_\-\-Error\-Code} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\hypertarget{group__Framework_ga58f4bdc1a05802f89005a487768b3d75}{\index{Framework@{Framework}!C\-U\-\_\-set\-\_\-error\-\_\-action@{C\-U\-\_\-set\-\_\-error\-\_\-action}}
\index{C\-U\-\_\-set\-\_\-error\-\_\-action@{C\-U\-\_\-set\-\_\-error\-\_\-action}!Framework@{Framework}}
\subsubsection[{C\-U\-\_\-set\-\_\-error\-\_\-action}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}C\-U\-\_\-\-E\-X\-P\-O\-R\-T void C\-U\-\_\-set\-\_\-error\-\_\-action (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf C\-U\-\_\-\-Error\-Action}}]{action}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{group__Framework_ga58f4bdc1a05802f89005a487768b3d75}


Sets the action to take when a framework error condition occurs. 

This function should be used to specify the action to take when an error condition is encountered. The default action is C\-U\-E\-A\-\_\-\-I\-G\-N\-O\-R\-E, which results in errors being ignored and test runs being continued (if possible). A value of C\-U\-E\-A\-\_\-\-F\-A\-I\-L causes test runs to stop as soon as an error condition occurs, while C\-U\-\_\-\-A\-B\-O\-R\-T causes the application to exit on any error.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Paramètres}
{\em action} & C\-U\-\_\-\-Error\-Action indicating the new error action. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{Voir également}
\hyperlink{group__Framework_gab2e98ce95448aa5a04a4875bc8152d6e}{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-error\-\_\-action()} 

\hyperlink{group__Framework_ga2e817abf46a330a699fe5f472f5bfd64}{C\-U\-\_\-set\-\_\-error()} 

\hyperlink{group__Framework_gab68a2bd9fee7d73f79c0cfc68c576b3a}{C\-U\-\_\-\-Error\-Action} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\hypertarget{group__Framework_ga39e01a31e7e84844f7cf5377d5cd8da2}{\index{Framework@{Framework}!C\-U\-\_\-set\-\_\-fail\-\_\-on\-\_\-inactive@{C\-U\-\_\-set\-\_\-fail\-\_\-on\-\_\-inactive}}
\index{C\-U\-\_\-set\-\_\-fail\-\_\-on\-\_\-inactive@{C\-U\-\_\-set\-\_\-fail\-\_\-on\-\_\-inactive}!Framework@{Framework}}
\subsubsection[{C\-U\-\_\-set\-\_\-fail\-\_\-on\-\_\-inactive}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}C\-U\-\_\-\-E\-X\-P\-O\-R\-T void C\-U\-\_\-set\-\_\-fail\-\_\-on\-\_\-inactive (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf C\-U\-\_\-\-B\-O\-O\-L}}]{new\-\_\-inactive}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{group__Framework_ga39e01a31e7e84844f7cf5377d5cd8da2}


Sets whether an inactive suite or test is treated as a failure. 

If C\-U\-\_\-\-T\-R\-U\-E, then failure records will be generated for inactive suites or tests encountered during a test run. The default is C\-U\-\_\-\-T\-R\-U\-E so that the client is reminded that the framewrork contains inactive suites/tests. Set to C\-U\-\_\-\-F\-A\-L\-S\-E to turn off this behavior.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Paramètres}
{\em new\-\_\-inactive} & New setting for whether to treat inactive suites and tests as failures during a test run (C\-U\-\_\-\-T\-R\-U\-E) or not (C\-U\-\_\-\-F\-A\-L\-S\-E). \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{Voir également}
C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-fail\-\_\-on\-\_\-failure() 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\hypertarget{group__Framework_gaaec6d8893d61bfff165775385851562d}{\index{Framework@{Framework}!C\-U\-\_\-set\-\_\-registry@{C\-U\-\_\-set\-\_\-registry}}
\index{C\-U\-\_\-set\-\_\-registry@{C\-U\-\_\-set\-\_\-registry}!Framework@{Framework}}
\subsubsection[{C\-U\-\_\-set\-\_\-registry}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}C\-U\-\_\-\-E\-X\-P\-O\-R\-T {\bf C\-U\-\_\-p\-Test\-Registry} C\-U\-\_\-set\-\_\-registry (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf C\-U\-\_\-p\-Test\-Registry}}]{p\-Test\-Registry}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{group__Framework_gaaec6d8893d61bfff165775385851562d}


Sets the registry to an existing C\-U\-\_\-p\-Test\-Registry instance. 

A pointer to the original registry is returned. Note that the original registry is not freed, and it becomes the caller's responsibility to do so. Directly accessing the registry should not be necessary for most users. This function is provided primarily for internal and testing purposes.\par
\par


{\bfseries This function must not be called during a test run (checked by assertion)}.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Renvoie}
A pointer to the original registry that was replaced. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{Voir également}
\hyperlink{group__Framework_ga3477b2d3e57c8f8aba36bbbdfa54920d}{C\-U\-\_\-initialize\-\_\-registry} 

\hyperlink{group__Framework_ga183eb7d7f79e149c767237cfef52cb82}{C\-U\-\_\-cleanup\-\_\-registry} 

\hyperlink{group__Framework_gacdc4bab7b0492ed1e3a4e076677de22e}{C\-U\-\_\-get\-\_\-registry} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\hypertarget{group__Framework_ga4e93ba1b139239e674b733fbab37988e}{\index{Framework@{Framework}!C\-U\-\_\-set\-\_\-suite\-\_\-active@{C\-U\-\_\-set\-\_\-suite\-\_\-active}}
\index{C\-U\-\_\-set\-\_\-suite\-\_\-active@{C\-U\-\_\-set\-\_\-suite\-\_\-active}!Framework@{Framework}}
\subsubsection[{C\-U\-\_\-set\-\_\-suite\-\_\-active}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}C\-U\-\_\-\-E\-X\-P\-O\-R\-T {\bf C\-U\-\_\-\-Error\-Code} C\-U\-\_\-set\-\_\-suite\-\_\-active (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf C\-U\-\_\-p\-Suite}}]{p\-Suite, }
\item[{{\bf C\-U\-\_\-\-B\-O\-O\-L}}]{f\-New\-Active}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{group__Framework_ga4e93ba1b139239e674b733fbab37988e}


Activates or deactivates a suite. 

Only activated suites can be executed during a test run. By default a suite is active upon creation, but can be deactivated by passing it along with C\-U\-\_\-\-F\-A\-L\-S\-E to this function. The suite can be reactivated by passing it along with C\-U\-\_\-\-T\-R\-U\-E. The current value of the active flag is available as p\-Suite-\/$>$f\-Active. If p\-Suite is N\-U\-L\-L then error code C\-U\-E\-\_\-\-N\-O\-S\-U\-I\-T\-E is returned.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Paramètres}
{\em p\-Suite} & Pointer to the suite to modify (non-\/\-N\-U\-L\-L). \\
\hline
{\em f\-New\-Active} & If C\-U\-\_\-\-T\-R\-U\-E then the suite will be activated; if C\-U\-\_\-\-F\-A\-L\-S\-E it will be deactivated. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Renvoie}

\hypertarget{group__Framework_gae13d2e11720784d22aa15713be90ce72}{\index{Framework@{Framework}!C\-U\-\_\-set\-\_\-test\-\_\-active@{C\-U\-\_\-set\-\_\-test\-\_\-active}}
\index{C\-U\-\_\-set\-\_\-test\-\_\-active@{C\-U\-\_\-set\-\_\-test\-\_\-active}!Framework@{Framework}}
\subsubsection[{C\-U\-\_\-set\-\_\-test\-\_\-active}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}C\-U\-\_\-\-E\-X\-P\-O\-R\-T {\bf C\-U\-\_\-\-Error\-Code} C\-U\-\_\-set\-\_\-test\-\_\-active (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf C\-U\-\_\-p\-Test}}]{p\-Test, }
\item[{{\bf C\-U\-\_\-\-B\-O\-O\-L}}]{f\-New\-Active}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{group__Framework_gae13d2e11720784d22aa15713be90ce72}


Activates or deactivates a specific test. 

Only activated tests can be executed during a test run. By default a test is active upon creation, but can be deactvated by passing it along with C\-U\-\_\-\-F\-A\-L\-S\-E to this function. The test can be reactivated by passing it along with C\-U\-\_\-\-T\-R\-U\-E. The current value of the active flag is available as p\-Test-\/$>$f\-Active. If p\-Test is N\-U\-L\-L then error code C\-U\-E\-\_\-\-N\-O\-T\-E\-S\-T is returned. Otherwise C\-U\-E\-\_\-\-S\-U\-C\-C\-E\-S\-S is returned.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Paramètres}
{\em p\-Test} & Pointer to the test to modify (non-\/\-N\-U\-L\-L). \\
\hline
{\em f\-New\-Active} & If C\-U\-\_\-\-T\-R\-U\-E then test will be activated; if C\-U\-\_\-\-F\-A\-L\-S\-E it will be deactivated. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Renvoie}
Returns C\-U\-E\-\_\-\-N\-O\-T\-E\-S\-T if p\-Test is N\-U\-L\-L, C\-U\-E\-\_\-\-S\-U\-C\-C\-E\-S\-S if all is well. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\hypertarget{group__Framework_ga24f4ea5ebafd70276bdc1bcdf1b89393}{\index{Framework@{Framework}!C\-U\-\_\-translate\-\_\-special\-\_\-characters@{C\-U\-\_\-translate\-\_\-special\-\_\-characters}}
\index{C\-U\-\_\-translate\-\_\-special\-\_\-characters@{C\-U\-\_\-translate\-\_\-special\-\_\-characters}!Framework@{Framework}}
\subsubsection[{C\-U\-\_\-translate\-\_\-special\-\_\-characters}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}C\-U\-\_\-\-E\-X\-P\-O\-R\-T size\-\_\-t C\-U\-\_\-translate\-\_\-special\-\_\-characters (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{const char $\ast$}]{sz\-Src, }
\item[{char $\ast$}]{sz\-Dest, }
\item[{size\-\_\-t}]{maxlen}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{group__Framework_ga24f4ea5ebafd70276bdc1bcdf1b89393}


Converts special characters in sz\-Src to xml entity codes and stores result in sz\-Dest. 

Currently conversion of '\&', '$<$', and '$>$' is supported. Note that conversion to entities increases the length of the converted string. The greatest conversion size increase would be a string consisting entirely of entity characters of converted length C\-U\-N\-I\-T\-\_\-\-M\-A\-X\-\_\-\-E\-N\-T\-I\-T\-Y\-\_\-\-L\-E\-N. Neither sz\-Src nor sz\-Dest may be N\-U\-L\-L (checked by assertion).\par
\par


maxlen gives the maximum number of characters in the translated string. If sz\-Dest does not have enough room to hold the converted string, the return value will be zero and sz\-Dest will contain an empty string. If this occurs, the remaining characters in sz\-Dest may be overwritten in an unspecified manner. It is the caller's responsibility to make sure there is sufficient room in sz\-Dest to hold the converted string. \hyperlink{group__Framework_gaed0d90c9fdd0c46b6043fb2b8ae570f4}{C\-U\-\_\-translated\-\_\-strlen()} may be used to calculate the length of buffer required (remember to add 1 for the terminating \textbackslash{}0).


\begin{DoxyParams}{Paramètres}
{\em sz\-Src} & Source string to convert (non-\/\-N\-U\-L\-L). \\
\hline
{\em sz\-Dest} & Location to hold the converted string (non-\/\-N\-U\-L\-L). \\
\hline
{\em maxlen} & Maximum number of characters sz\-Dest can hold. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Renvoie}
The number of special characters converted (always 0 if sz\-Dest did not have enough room to hold converted string). 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\hypertarget{group__Framework_gaed0d90c9fdd0c46b6043fb2b8ae570f4}{\index{Framework@{Framework}!C\-U\-\_\-translated\-\_\-strlen@{C\-U\-\_\-translated\-\_\-strlen}}
\index{C\-U\-\_\-translated\-\_\-strlen@{C\-U\-\_\-translated\-\_\-strlen}!Framework@{Framework}}
\subsubsection[{C\-U\-\_\-translated\-\_\-strlen}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}C\-U\-\_\-\-E\-X\-P\-O\-R\-T size\-\_\-t C\-U\-\_\-translated\-\_\-strlen (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{const char $\ast$}]{sz\-Src}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{group__Framework_gaed0d90c9fdd0c46b6043fb2b8ae570f4}


Calculates the length of a translated string. 

This function calculates the buffer length required to hold a string after processing with \hyperlink{group__Framework_ga24f4ea5ebafd70276bdc1bcdf1b89393}{C\-U\-\_\-translate\-\_\-special\-\_\-characters()}. The returned length does not include space for the terminating '\textbackslash{}0' character. sz\-Src may not be N\-U\-L\-L (checked by assertion).


\begin{DoxyParams}{Paramètres}
{\em sz\-Src} & Source string to analyze (non-\/\-N\-U\-L\-L). \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Renvoie}
The number of characters sz\-Src will expand to when converted. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\hypertarget{group__Framework_gab4f507101595640f759647d13f0e0a00}{\index{Framework@{Framework}!C\-U\-\_\-trim@{C\-U\-\_\-trim}}
\index{C\-U\-\_\-trim@{C\-U\-\_\-trim}!Framework@{Framework}}
\subsubsection[{C\-U\-\_\-trim}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}C\-U\-\_\-\-E\-X\-P\-O\-R\-T void C\-U\-\_\-trim (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}

\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{group__Framework_gab4f507101595640f759647d13f0e0a00}


Trims leading and trailing whitespace from the specified string. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Paramètres}

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\hypertarget{group__Framework_gade303bc81f692aa882189eb14484be8f}{\index{Framework@{Framework}!C\-U\-\_\-trim\-\_\-left@{C\-U\-\_\-trim\-\_\-left}}
\index{C\-U\-\_\-trim\-\_\-left@{C\-U\-\_\-trim\-\_\-left}!Framework@{Framework}}
\subsubsection[{C\-U\-\_\-trim\-\_\-left}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}C\-U\-\_\-\-E\-X\-P\-O\-R\-T void C\-U\-\_\-trim\-\_\-left (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{char $\ast$}]{sz\-String}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{group__Framework_gade303bc81f692aa882189eb14484be8f}


Trims leading whitespace from the specified string. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Paramètres}
{\em sz\-String} & The string to trim. \\
